 CCTV cameras installed at 17 stations of Konkan Railway
 CCTV cameras installed at 17 stations of Konkan Railway are of state-of-the-art technology
 steshnon par get, lobby, plateform, tikat booking windo se lekar tamaam aisi jagahon parasisitivicamare lagaae gaye hai, jahaan par yatriyon or railway karmchaariyon kii awajahi he

 2
